msg:I started looking at hotel information in 2018 and was worried that the hotel facilities were too old.

When I arrived at the hotel, the overall feeling was very good. The lobby was very large and heated! There are ground and underground parking lots.

Service: The ladies and brothers at the front desk are very good. They will help pick up and drop off luggage. They will also introduce nearby tourist attractions and food. Because of the New Year, the hotel also has a scenic spot check-in event for tourists. If you collect enough scenic spot check-in photos, you can go to the hotel to exchange gifts. This is very good. In this way, children will be very active in taking photos and checking in. Originally, only one can be exchanged, but because our two children have a special application for an extra Red Army backpack.

Facilities: Although the hotel is quite old, the facilities inside are quite new and obviously renovated. There is a children's playground next to the front desk, and a robot food delivery service is equipped! There is a heated swimming pool and a gym on the third floor. The most satisfactory thing about the room is that there is a cloakroom and a large bathtub, and the bathing and toilet are separated! This price is also great value during the Chinese New Year. I have a small suggestion that the pillow is too soft. It would be better if there is an extra hard pillow~

RestaurantğŸ´: The restaurant is on the first floor. The breakfast is very rich. There are all kinds of cakes, flour, soup, and tofu pudding~ You can season the salty and sweet ones yourselfğŸ§‚, which satisfies the Guangdong stomachğŸ‘!

Both the hardware and software meet the needs of families with children, so we immediately extended the room for one more day. It is a five-star hotel with a three-star price. If I have the opportunity to travel to Nanchang again, I will continue to choose it!

One regret is that I did not receive the New Year souvenirs and the additional check-in fruit service~
